Spring and Autumn

After Foreign Firms’ Tea Business Stopped Exchange, Business Federation and Others Sent Representatives to Petition, Qian Chengxu Took the Petition to Nanjing to Transfer it to the Executive Yuan, and Met with Liu Zhenhua to Investigate the Actual Situation 102

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce and the China General Chamber of Industry, due to Anhui Province’s implementation of centralized control of black tea, resulting in the closure of tea warehouses and the cessation of exchange, various places in Anhui and Jiangxi provinces sent telegrams to appeal. On the 15th, a joint meeting was held, and it was decided to send Qian Chengxu to Anhui to meet with Chairman Liu Zhenhua to specifically discuss the issues of centralized control and the cessation of exchange. The details are as follows:

Qian’s Speech: Qian Chengxu, the representative sent by the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce and the China General Chamber of Industry, took a train to Nanjing from Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., and then went to Anqing to meet with Liu Zhenhua, Chairman of Anhui Province. According to Qian’s pre-departure statement, “My task in going to Anhui this time is entrusted by the two associations. Regarding the recent tea business in Anhui, as well as the two issues of exporting abroad, I will discuss with the authorities a method that is more suitable for the actual situation, so that it can increase soundness and fully exert its strength in the organization of the national economy at home and abroad. It is found that in recent years, China’s tea production has been squeezed by foreign tea, and the original overseas markets have been gradually seized by foreign tea. If the quality is not improved, it will undoubtedly decline more and more over time. Therefore, many enthusiastic industrialists in the country are running around calling for reform and feelings, and various writings can be seen on the recent situation in Anhui, or because of this relationship, there is its motive. However, tea has become an industry in China, and there are many places where it is related to the industry and commerce in various parts of the country. The export of tens of millions of dollars every year is enough to be an authoritative tool for balancing international trade, and its economic organization background is formed by the aggregation of various cellular components. For example, the tea warehouse is also one of the physical organizations, and its position is between the tea firm and the foreign merchant. It is in the position of a broker and represents both parties, each bearing its own responsibilities and guarantees. Today’s tea industry situation has not changed much in terms of transaction procedures compared to 30 years ago. The psychological trust of foreign merchants in tea warehouses can still be maintained. Therefore, once the organization is changed, whether the new organization can bear this heavy burden and whether it can gain the trust of foreign merchants are all questions. This is also the point that we should pay attention to. “The reporter asked, “What is the method to improve its organization?” Qian replied, “The scope of this section is very broad and cannot be answered in a short period of time. Choosing its main points, according to the main views and principles of the two associations, it has always been believed that the first step of unified control of products should be to improve the quality of the producing area as a prerequisite, and the sales part should still be operated by merchants, which is appropriate and easy to adjust in production and sales. Because merchants have a keen sense of cherishing and saving every penny of their own blood capital, so their expenses are not wasteful and are properly used. Even in the scope of business with no great profit, some profit can still be obtained due to proper business calculations. As for government-run enterprises, it is not to say that those who are in charge are all irresponsible people, but because their business knowledge is insufficient, and most of their parents are not from the business community, so they are separated by circumstances, or because of the lack of various connections, they end up with inflexible skills, and as a result, bad effects occur. Therefore, as soon as I arrive in Anhui, I plan to present the facts to the authorities in the province to seek understanding, but it is difficult to predict whether the goal can be achieved.”

The Petition of the Two Associations: Qian also carried the joint petition of the two associations to be submitted to Chairman Liu. The original text said, "Chairman Liu of the Anhui Provincial Government, the cessation of exchange of tea warehouses directly affects foreign trade and indirectly hinders domestic agriculture and commerce. At this time when the export of domestic tea is declining, occasionally due to system changes, it is not entirely appropriate, or because the timing is not yet ripe, it has been hit hard. The loss is not only the province that bears the brunt, but also the national economy and national industrial and commercial enterprises will also be affected, needless to say. Our association has witnessed the difficulties of the times, and believes that in the national economic organization, most of the old systems are not in line with modern trends, but they have been used for thousands of years, and their operation is still lively. There is a central force and a special environment, mutual communication, mutual attraction and mutual generation, and the spirit of the country and the relationship with foreign countries are entrusted to it. In short, the old system of China’s economic organization should take the promotion of its improvement and cooperation as a prerequisite. Overly radical behavior will lead to the disadvantage of wanting to be quick but not achieving the goal. Observing the recent realities in various provinces is enough to prove it. Now that your government is in charge of tea production, it is heard that it is being operated by a specially established agency. Shanghai tea warehouse merchants have stopped exchange due to misunderstandings. The domestic economy is on the verge of collapse, and foreign supply is also cut off. Our association believes that the timing is urgent and it is not appropriate to remain silent. Therefore, after a joint meeting, it was decided to publicly elect Qian Chengxu to make a special trip to pay respects to investigate the actual situation and make appropriate suggestions so that the current method is more suitable for the actual situation. We respectfully request to be granted an audience and guidance. This is what we hope for. Guo Shun, Chairman of the China General Chamber of Industry, and Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, respectfully kowtow."

Continued Cessation of Exchange: The 14 tea warehouses including Zhongxin Chang and others of the Foreign Firms Tea Industry Association have been closed for many days due to their opposition to Anhui Province’s unified control of Qihong tea and the implementation of cessation of exchange and business. The tea warehouses in Anhui and Jiangxi provinces have stopped exchange, affecting the finances of Anhui and Jiangxi provinces. In addition, hundreds of thousands of tea farmers, tea workers, and tea merchants have been greatly affected. They have sent telegrams to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, requesting that the tea warehouses be ordered to exchange drafts to reassure people. Yesterday, I inquired about the Foreign Firms Tea Industry Association to see if there was any indication of resumption of exchange. According to the spokesperson of the association, "The purpose of our association is all expressed in the official statement. Now we have decided to wait quietly for the instructions of Director Jiang and the competent authorities. Before a real solution is obtained, we have decided to continue the cessation of exchange."

Shanghai Maritime Administration Bureau Urges Improvement of Escort Equipment, Deadline for Detailed Reporting within Ten Days 103

The Shanghai Maritime Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, in view of the fact that the sea navigation and security equipment of the various wheels traveling on the inner and outer rivers are dilapidated, and in the event of incidents such as bandits riding robbery or unexpected wind and rain, there is no way to ensure the safety of passengers, and the loss of goods and the death of passengers are often heard. Now, the state-owned China Merchants Bureau and the privately-owned Sanbei, Ningshao, Datong, Dazhen and other larger shipping companies in the port have gradually improved all the escort equipment of the ships traveling on the near-sea, ocean, Yangtze River lines, etc., so the number of accidents has gradually decreased. However, most shipping companies still have to simplify the equipment due to capital relations, which is contrary to the maritime regulations. The bureau has recently received an order from the Ministry of Communications to strictly urge the various shipping companies to improve the escort equipment. Now the bureau has printed forms, which will be distributed to the various wheel companies, and all the companies are required to fill them out and report them to the bureau within ten days from the date of the document for review and handling. The bureau will try to improve the equipment according to the situation of each wheel, otherwise it will be banned.

Embassies of Japan, Germany, and Poland in China are Preparing to Celebrate Anniversaries, Japan Celebrates Emperor’s Birthday, Germany and Poland Celebrate National Day 104

The 29th of this month is the Emperor’s Birthday in Japan. The Japanese Embassy in China has decided to hold celebrations in Beijing and Tianjin on this day, and prepare champagne, tea, and refreshments to entertain guests. The 1st of next month is the German Republic Memorial Day. The German Ambassador has also decided to hold a celebration on this day, but it is heard that he does not intend to entertain foreign guests. Also, the 2nd of next month is the Polish National Day Anniversary. The Polish Ambassador to China, Wei Dentao, has decided to hold a grand tea party at the Capital Hotel on this day to entertain guests.

Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Kita Holds Tea Party Tonight to Entertain Chinese and Japanese Officials for a Social Gathering 105

According to Shen Shi News, after Major General Kita Seiichi, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy in China, took office in Shanghai, he has already visited Mayor Wu and Commander Yang, and is scheduled to go to Tianjin from Shanghai on the 30th of this month to visit Foreign Minister Zhang, Minister of Military Affairs He, and various important figures in the central military and political circles. According to news from the Japanese Embassy, Kita has decided to hold a tea party at the Japanese Club on Peng Road at 6 p.m. today to entertain Chinese and Japanese officials from all parties for a social gathering.
